style="display:inline-block;user-select:none;vertical-align:text-bottom;overflow:visible"><path d="M5.75 2.5h8.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-8.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5Zm0 5h8.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-8.5a.75.75 0 0 class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 react-blob-header-edit-and-raw-actions-combined"><button data-component="IconButton" type="button" aria-label="Edit and raw actions" class="types__StyledButton-sc-ws60qy-0 dGDIQc js-blob-dropdown-click" title="More file actions" data-testid="more-file-actions-button" id=":Rnsptal9laeb:" aria-haspopup="true" tabindex="0" data-size="small" data-no-visuals="true"><svg 0 0-3 1.5 1.5 0 0 0 0 3Z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 ytOJl"><section aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eRvpKx"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 cTsUqU js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">netwatcher设计文档</h1><a id="user-content-netwatcher设计文档" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: netwatcher设计文档" href="#netwatcher设计文档"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>本文详细说明netwatcher的代码设计</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">监控流程</h2><a id="user-content-监控流程" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 监控流程" href="#监控流程"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/linuxkerneltravel/lmp/blob/develop/eBPF_Supermarket/Network_Subsystem/net_watcher/doc/image/process.png"><img src="/linuxkerneltravel/lmp/raw/develop/eBPF_Supermarket/Network_Subsystem/net_watcher/doc/image/process.png" alt="监控流程图" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">如图所示，<code>netwatcher</code>监控每个建立的TCP连接与各个连接上的数据包：</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>当TCP连接建立时，<code>netwatcher</code>记录下此TCP连接的基本信息，即连接id,连接socket地址,相关COMMAND,连接四元组以及连接方向</li>
<li>当数据包到来时，<code>netwatcher</code>首先记录此数据包的基础信息，即SEQ,ACK,TCP包sock地址（用于明确TCP连接），接着根据指定参数
<ul dir="auto">
<li>记录数据包的额外信息</li>
<li>更新相关TCP连接的额外信息</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">数据结构</h2><a id="user-content-数据结构" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 数据结构" href="#数据结构"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">kernal struct</h3><a id="user-content-kernal-struct" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kernal struct" href="#kernal-struct"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>struct ktime_info</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>记录每个包到达各层的时间戳</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>packet_tuple</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>记录tcp包核心信息，以供辅助函数使用</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">user struct</h3><a id="user-content-user-struct" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: user struct" href="#user-struct"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>struct sonn_t</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>tcp连接相关信息</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>struct pack_t</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>tcp包相关信息</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">eBPF MAP</h3><a id="user-content-ebpf-map" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: eBPF MAP" href="#ebpf-map"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>BPF_MAP_TYPE_LRU_HASH timestamps</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>key: <code>struct packet_tuple</code></li>
<li>value: <code>struct ktime_info</code></li>
<li>存储每个包所对应的<code>ktime_info</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>BPF_MAP_TYPE_RINGBUF rb</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>包相关信息通过此buffer提供给user space</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>BPF_MAP_TYPE_LRU_HASH conns_info</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>key: <code>struct sock *</code></li>
<li>value: <code>conn_t</code></li>
<li>存储每个tcp连接所对应的<code>conn_t</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>BPF_MAP_TYPE_LRU_HASH sock_stores</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>key: <code>u64 ptid</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>value: <code>struct sock*</code></li>
<li>根据<code>ptid</code>存储<code>sock</code>指针，从而在上下文无<code>sock</code>的内核探测点获得<code>sock</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">kernel space探测</h2><a id="user-content-kernel-space探测" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kernel space探测" href="#kernel-space探测"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">APP层</h3><a id="user-content-app层" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: APP层" href="#app层"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>kprobe/skb_copy_datagram_iter</code></h4><a id="user-content-kprobeskb_copy_datagram_iter" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kprobe/skb_copy_datagram_iter" href="#kprobeskb_copy_datagram_iter"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>rx数据包经过TCP层处理后进入此函数</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>记录rx数据包到达APP层的时间戳，存入<code>timestamps</code></li>
<li>根据<code>timestamps</code>中的时间戳计算数据包的各层处理时间</li>
<li>从<code>sock</code>中提取出用户数据，从而供user space提取出HTTP1/1.1请求头</li>
<li>将数据包相关信息存入<code>rb</code>以供user space消费</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">TCP层</h3><a id="user-content-tcp层" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: TCP层" href="#tcp层"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>kretprobe/inet_csk_accept</code></h4><a id="user-content-kretprobeinet_csk_accept" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kretprobe/inet_csk_accept" href="#kretprobeinet_csk_accept"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>accept()</code>系统调用最终会调用此函数，成功后此函数会返回一个<code>struct sock* sk</code>，此<code>sk</code>管理着被accept的tcp连接</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>根据<code>sk</code>记录tcp连接的基本信息并存入<code>conns_info</code></li>
<li>由于是accept，将conn的方向设为server</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>kprobe/tcp_v4/v6_connect</code></h4><a id="user-content-kprobetcp_v4v6_connect" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kprobe/tcp_v4/v6_connect" href="#kprobetcp_v4v6_connect"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>connect(struct sock* sk)</code>系统调用最终会调用此函数</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>记录<code>ptid</code>与<code>sk</code>的对应关系，并存入<code>sock_stores</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>kretprobe/tcp_v4/v6_connect</code></h4><a id="user-content-kretprobetcp_v4v6_connect" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kretprobe/tcp_v4/v6_connect" href="#kretprobetcp_v4v6_connect"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>connect(struct sock* sk)</code>系统调用最终会调用此函数</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>根据<code>kprobe</code>中记录的信息，将tcp连接的基本信息存入<code>conns_info</code></li>
<li>由于是connect，将conn的方向设为client</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>kprobe/tcp_set_state</code></h4><a id="user-content-kprobetcp_set_state" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kprobe/tcp_set_state" href="#kprobetcp_set_state"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>每次tcp连接状态发生变化会调用此函数</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>若未指定运行参数<code>-a</code>，则当tcp连接状态变为<code>TCP_CLOSE</code>时，将此tcp连接信息从<code>sock_stores</code>与<code>conns_info</code>中删去（如果有的话）</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>kprobe/tcp_v4/v6_rcv</code></h4><a id="user-content-kprobetcp_v4v6_rcv" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kprobe/tcp_v4/v6_rcv" href="#kprobetcp_v4v6_rcv"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>当rx数据包到达TCP层时，会调用此函数</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>记录IP数据包到达TCP层的时间戳，存入<code>timestamps</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>tcp_v4/v6_do_rcv</code></h4><a id="user-content-tcp_v4v6_do_rcv" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: tcp_v4/v6_do_rcv" href="#tcp_v4v6_do_rcv"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>tcp_v4/v6_rcv</code>在此函数进一步处理rx包</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>根据<code>sock</code>得到<code>tcp_sock</code>，更新tcp连接的额外信息到相应的<code>conn_t</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>kprobe/tcp_validate_incoming</code></h4><a id="user-content-kprobetcp_validate_incoming" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kprobe/tcp_validate_incoming" href="#kprobetcp_validate_incoming"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>linux协议栈使用此函数对tcp包进行校验</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>校验TCP包seq是否在接收窗口中</li>
<li>如果TCP包seq错误，将此包相关信息存入<code>rb</code>以供user space消费</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>kretprobe/__skb_checksum_complete</code></h4><a id="user-content-kretprobe__skb_checksum_complete" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kretprobe/__skb_checksum_complete" href="#kretprobe__skb_checksum_complete"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>此函数返回非0表明数据包校验和错误</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>对校验和错误的数据包相关信息存入<code>rb</code>以供user space消费</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>kprobe/tcp_sendmsg</code></h4><a id="user-content-kprobetcp_sendmsg" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kprobe/tcp_sendmsg" href="#kprobetcp_sendmsg"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>linux协议栈在TCP层调用此函数对tx包进行处理</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>记录tx包到达TCP层的时间戳</li>
<li>根据<code>sock</code>得到<code>tcp_sock</code>，更新tcp连接的额外信息到相应的<code>conn_t</code></li>
<li>从<code>struct msghdr* msg</code>中提取用户层数据，从而供user space提取出HTTP1/1.1请求头</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>kprobe/dev_hard_start_xmit</code></h4><a id="user-content-kprobedev_hard_start_xmit" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: kprobe/dev_hard_start_xmit" href="#kprobedev_hard_start_xmit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>linux协议栈调用此函数将tx数据包发送给网卡驱动</li>
<li>netwatcher在此探测点做出如下动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>记录tx数据包离开MAC层的时间戳，存入<code>timestamps</code></li>
<li>将数据包相关信息存入<code>rb</code>以供user space消费</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">user space 输出</h2><a id="user-content-user-space-输出" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: user space 输出" href="#user-space-输出"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">连接相关信息</h3><a id="user-content-连接相关信息" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 连接相关信息" href="#连接相关信息"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>netwatcher通过<code>bpf_map_get_next_key</code>对<code>conns_info</code>进行遍历，将其中存储的所有TCP连接信息按如下格式输出到<code>data/connects.log</code>文件中</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fprintf(file, &quot;connection{pid=\&quot;%d\&quot;,sock=\&quot;%p\&quot;,src=\&quot;%s\&quot;,dst=\&quot;%s\&quot;,is_server=\&quot;%d\&quot;&quot;,
d.pid, d.sock, s_ip_port_str, d_ip_port_str, d.is_server);"><pre class="notranslate"><code>fprintf(file, "connection{pid=\"%d\",sock=\"%p\",src=\"%s\",dst=\"%s\",is_server=\"%d\"",
d.pid, d.sock, s_ip_port_str, d_ip_port_str, d.is_server);
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">数据包相关信息</h3><a id="user-content-数据包相关信息" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 数据包相关信息" href="#数据包相关信息"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>数据包相关信息首先以如下格式输出至标准输出</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="printf(&quot;%-22s %-10s %-10s %-10s %-10s %-10s %-5s %s\n&quot;,
 &quot;SOCK&quot;, &quot;SEQ&quot;, &quot;ACK&quot;, &quot;MAC_TIME&quot;, &quot;IP_TIME&quot;, &quot;TCP_TIME&quot;, &quot;RX&quot;, &quot;HTTP&quot;);"><pre class="notranslate"><code>printf("%-22s %-10s %-10s %-10s %-10s %-10s %-5s %s\n",
 "SOCK", "SEQ", "ACK", "MAC_TIME", "IP_TIME", "TCP_TIME", "RX", "HTTP");
</code></pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>数据包相关信息还以如下格式输出至<code>data/packets.log</code>中</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fprintf(file,&quot;packet{sock=\&quot;%p\&quot;,seq=\&quot;%u\&quot;,ack=\&quot;%u\&quot;,mac_time=\&quot;%llu\&quot;,ip_time=\&quot;%llu\&quot;,tcp_time=\&quot;%llu\&quot;,http_info=\&quot;%s\&quot;,rx=\&quot;%d\&quot;} 0\n&quot;,
pack_info-&gt;sock, pack_info-&gt;seq, pack_info-&gt;ack, pack_info-&gt;mac_time, pack_info-&gt;ip_time, pack_info-&gt;tcp_time, http_data, pack_info-&gt;rx);"><pre class="notranslate"><code>fprintf(file,"packet{sock=\"%p\",seq=\"%u\",ack=\"%u\",mac_time=\"%llu\",ip_time=\"%llu\",tcp_time=\"%llu\",http_info=\"%s\",rx=\"%d\"} 0\n",
pack_info-&gt;sock, pack_info-&gt;seq, pack_info-&gt;ack, pack_info-&gt;mac_time, pack_info-&gt;ip_time, pack_info-&gt;tcp_time, http_data, pack_info-&gt;rx);
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">数据包错误</h3><a id="user-content-数据包错误" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 数据包错误" href="#数据包错误"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>数据包错误信息首先以如下格式输出至标准输出</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="printf(&quot;[X] invalid SEQ: sock = %p,seq= %u,ack = %u\n&quot;,
                   pack_info-&gt;sock, pack_info-&gt;seq, pack_info-&gt;ack);
printf(&quot;[X] invalid checksum: sock = %p\n&quot;, pack_info-&gt;sock);"><pre class="notranslate"><code>printf("[X] invalid SEQ: sock = %p,seq= %u,ack = %u\n",
                   pack_info-&gt;sock, pack_info-&gt;seq, pack_info-&gt;ack);
printf("[X] invalid checksum: sock = %p\n", pack_info-&gt;sock);
</code></pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>数据包错误信息还以如下格式输出至<code>data/err.log</code>中</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fprintf(file, &quot;error{sock=\&quot;%p\&quot;,seq=\&quot;%u\&quot;,ack=\&quot;%u\&quot;,reason=\&quot;%s\&quot;} 0\n&quot;,
pack_info-&gt;sock, pack_info-&gt;seq, pack_info-&gt;ack, reason);"><pre class="notranslate"><code>fprintf(file, "error{sock=\"%p\",seq=\"%u\",ack=\"%u\",reason=\"%s\"} 0\n",
pack_info-&gt;sock, pack_info-&gt;seq, pack_info-&gt;ack, reason);
</code></pre></div>
